Dataset {i}/5, Method {j}/3, ECE={current_ece:.4f}\\\")\\n  ```\\n\\n**Early Stopping:**\\n- If ECE for all methods is within 0.01 on 2 consecutive datasets, TEC unlikely to help\\n- If GPU memory error occurs, switch to CPU fallback\\n- If time exceeds 5 hours, stop and save partial results\",\n  \"metadata\": {\n    \"experiment_type\": \"calibration_evaluation\",\n    \"methods\": [\"uncalibrated\", \"temperature_scaling\", \"thermodynamic_entropy_calibration\"],\n    \"datasets\": [\"sst-2\", \"qnli\", \"ag_news\", \"mnli\", \"dbpedia\"],\n    \"primary_metric\": \"expected_calibration_error\",\n    \"secondary_metrics\": [\"brier_score\", \"negative_log_likelihood\", \"accuracy\"],\n    \"statistical_test\": \"bootstrap_confidence_interval\",\n    \"n_bootstrap\": 1000,\n    \"heterogeneous_analysis\": true,\n    \"time_budget_hours\": 6\n  }\n}", "new_content": "{\n  \"title\": \"Test TEC vs TS Calibration on 5 LLM Datasets\",\n  \"summary\": \"Compare thermodynamic entropy calibration and temperature scaling on SST-2, QNLI, AG News, MNLI, DBpedia using pre-trained transformers. Evaluate on heterogeneous splits with bootstrap CI.\",\n  \"runpod_compute_profile\": \"gpu\",\n  \"implementation_pseudocode\": \"## Experimental Setup\\n\\n### Dataset Preparation\\n1. Load the standardized datasets from the dependency artifact (full_data_out.json)\\n2. For each dataset, load the appropriate pre-trained model:\\n   - SST-2: distilbert-base-uncased-finetuned-sst-2-english\\n   - QNLI: distilbert-base-uncased-finetuned-sst-2-english (or BERT-base)\\n   - AG News: roberta-base (fine-tuned on AG News)\\n   - MNLI: roberta-large-mnli (or roberta-base)\\n   - DBpedia: bert-base-uncased (fine-tuned on DBpedia)\\n3. Split each dataset into:\\n   - Train (60%): for model fine-tuning if needed\\n   - Validation (20%): for hyperparameter tuning\\n   - Test (20%): for final evaluation\\n\\n### Model & Logit Extraction\\n```python\\nimport torch\\nfrom transformers import AutoModelForSequenceClassification, AutoTokenizer\\nfrom torch.utils.data import DataLoader\\nimport json\\n\\n# Load dataset\\nwith open('full_data_out.json', 'r') as f:\\n    data = json.load(f)\\n\\n# Model mapping\\ndataset_models = {\\n    'sst-2': 'distilbert-base-uncased-finetuned-sst-2-english',\\n    'qnli': 'bert-base-uncased',  # May need QNLI fine-tuned version\\n    'ag_news': 'roberta-base',  # May need AG News fine-tuned\\n    'mnli': 'roberta-large-mnli',\\n    'dbpedia': 'bert-base-uncased'  # May need DBpedia fine-tuned\\n}\\n\\n# Extract logits for each dataset\\nfor dataset_name, model_name in dataset_models.items():\\n    tokenizer = AutoTokenizer.from_pretrained(model_name)\\n    model = AutoModelForSequenceClassification.from_pretrained(model_name)\\n    model.eval()\\n    \\n    # Get dataset examples\\n    dataset = [d for d in data['datasets'] if d['dataset'] == dataset_name][0]\\n    examples = dataset['examples']\\n    \\n    # Extract logits (no gradient)\\n    with torch.no_grad():\\n        for ex in examples:\\n            inputs = tokenizer(ex['input'], return_tensors='pt', truncation=True, padding=True)\\n            outputs = model(**inputs)\\n            logits = outputs.logits\\n            # Store logits with example\\n            ex['logits'] = logits.numpy().tolist()\\n            ex['num_classes'] = logits.shape[-1]\\n```\\n\\n### Method 1: Uncalibrated Baseline\\n```python\\ndef uncalibrated_predictions(logits):\\n    # Softmax without temperature scaling\\n    probs = torch.softmax(torch.tensor(logits), dim=-1)\\n    preds = torch.argmax(probs, dim=-1)\\n    confs = torch.max(probs, dim=-1).values\\n    return preds, confs, probs\\n```\\n\\n### Method 2: Temperature Scaling (TS)\\n```python\\nimport torch.nn as nn\\nimport torch.optim as optim\\n\\ndef temperature_scaling(logits, labels, val_logits, val_labels):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Tune temperature T on validation set to minimize NLL.\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    # Initialize temperature\\n    temperature = nn.Parameter(torch.ones(1) * 1.0)\\n    optimizer = optim.LBFGS([temperature], lr=0.01, max_iter=50)\\n    \\n    logits_tensor = torch.tensor(logits)\\n    labels_tensor = torch.tensor(labels)\\n    \\n    def eval():\\n        optimizer.zero_grad()\\n        scaled_logits = logits_tensor / temperature\\n        loss = nn.CrossEntropyLoss()(scaled_logits, labels_tensor)\\n        loss.backward()\\n        return loss\\n    \\n    # Optimize temperature\\n    for _ in range(100):\\n        optimizer.step(eval)\\n    \\n    # Apply to validation set\\n    with torch.no_grad():\\n        val_scaled = torch.tensor(val_logits) / temperature\\n        val_probs = torch.softmax(val_scaled, dim=-1)\\n        val_preds = torch.argmax(val_probs, dim=-1)\\n        val_confs = torch.max(val_probs, dim=-1).values\\n    \\n    return temperature.item(), val_preds, val_confs, val_probs\\n```\\n\\n### Method 3: Thermodynamic Entropy Calibration (TEC)\\n```python\\ndef compute_entropy(probs):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Compute Shannon entropy of probability distribution.\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    epsilon = 1e-12\\n    probs = torch.clamp(probs, epsilon, 1.0 - epsilon)\\n    entropy = -torch.sum(probs * torch.log(probs), dim=-1)\\n    return entropy\\n\\ndef compute_margin(probs):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Compute decision margin (difference between top-2 predictions).\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    sorted_probs, _ = torch.sort(probs, dim=-1, descending=True)\\n    margin = sorted_probs[..., 0] - sorted_probs[..., 1]\\n    return margin\\n\\ndef tec_calibration(logits, T_0, alpha, beta):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Thermodynamic Entropy Calibration.\\n    \\n    Adjusts per-sample temperature based on entropy and margin:\\n    T_sample = T_0 * (1 + alpha * entropy - beta * margin)\\n    \\n    Args:\\n        logits: Raw logits (N, C)\\n        T_0: Base temperature parameter\\n        alpha: Entropy weight parameter\\n        beta: Margin weight parameter\\n    \\n    Returns:\\n        Calibrated probabilities\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    probs = torch.softmax(torch.tensor(logits), dim=-1)\\n    entropy = compute_entropy(probs)\\n    margin = compute_margin(probs)\\n    \\n    # Normalize entropy and margin to [0, 1]\\n    max_entropy = torch.log(torch.tensor(probs.shape[-1]).float())\\n    norm_entropy = entropy / max_entropy\\n    norm_margin = margin  # Already in [0, 1]\\n    \\n    # Compute per-sample temperature\\n    T_sample = T_0 * (1 + alpha * norm_entropy - beta * norm_margin)\\n    T_sample = torch.clamp(T_sample, min=0.01, max=100.0)  # Prevent extremes\\n    \\n    # Apply temperature scaling per sample\\n    # Need to handle per-sample temperature\\n    scaled_logits = torch.tensor(logits) / T_sample.unsqueeze(-1)\\n    calibrated_probs = torch.softmax(scaled_logits, dim=-1)\\n    \\n    return calibrated_probs, T_sample\\n\\ndef tune_tec_hyperparameters(val_logits, val_labels):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Grid search for TEC hyperparameters.\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    best_ece = float('inf')\\n    best_params = None\\n    \\n    T_0_range = [0.1, 0.5, 1.0, 2.0, 5.0, 10.0, 20.0]\\n    alpha_range = [0.0, 0.5, 1.0, 1.5, 2.0]\\n    beta_range = [0.0, 0.25, 0.5, 0.75, 1.0]\\n    \\n    for T_0 in T_0_range:\\n        for alpha in alpha_range:\\n            for beta in beta_range:\\n                probs, _ = tec_calibration(val_logits, T_0, alpha, beta)\\n                ece = compute_ece(probs, val_labels)\\n                \\n                if ece < best_ece:\\n                    best_ece = ece\\n                    best_params = (T_0, alpha, beta)\\n    \\n    return best_params, best_ece\\n```\\n\\n### Heterogeneous Split Creation\\n```python\\ndef create_heterogeneous_splits(logits, labels, easy_ratio=0.5):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Split dataset into easy (high margin) and hard (low margin) examples.\\n    \\n    Args:\\n        logits: Raw logits\\n        labels: True labels\\n        easy_ratio: Ratio of easy examples to include\\n    \\n    Returns:\\n        easy_indices, hard_indices\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    probs = torch.softmax(torch.tensor(logits), dim=-1)\\n    margin = compute_margin(probs)\\n    \\n    # Sort by margin\\n    sorted_indices = torch.argsort(margin, descending=True)\\n    \\n    n_easy = int(len(sorted_indices) * easy_ratio)\\n    easy_indices = sorted_indices[:n_easy]\\n    hard_indices = sorted_indices[n_easy:]\\n    \\n    return easy_indices, hard_indices\\n```\\n\\n### Metrics Computation\\n```python\\nimport numpy as np\\nfrom sklearn.metrics import brier_score_loss\\n\\ndef compute_ece(probs, labels, n_bins=10):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Compute Expected Calibration Error.\\n    \\n    Args:\\n        probs: Predicted probabilities (N, C)\\n        labels: True labels (N,)\\n        n_bins: Number of bins for calibration\\n    \\n    Returns:\\n        ECE value\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    # Get confidence and predictions\\n    confs = torch.max(probs, dim=-1).values.numpy()\\n    preds = torch.argmax(probs, dim=-1).numpy()\\n    labels = np.array(labels)\\n    \\n    # Bin predictions\\n    bins = np.linspace(0, 1, n_bins + 1)\\n    ece = 0.0\\n    \\n    for i in range(n_bins):\\n        mask = (confs >= bins[i]) & (confs < bins[i + 1])\\n        if mask.sum() > 0:\\n            bin_acc = np.mean(preds[mask] == labels[mask])\\n            bin_conf = np.mean(confs[mask])\\n            ece += np.abs(bin_acc - bin_conf) * mask.sum() / len(confs)\\n    \\n    return ece\\n\\ndef compute_nll(probs, labels):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Compute Negative Log-Likelihood.\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    probs = torch.clamp(probs, min=1e-12, max=1.0)\\n    labels = torch.tensor(labels)\\n    nll = -torch.log(probs[torch.arange(len(labels)), labels]).mean()\\n    return nll.item()\\n\\ndef compute_brier_score(probs, labels, n_classes):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Compute Brier Score.\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    # One-hot encode labels\\n    labels_onehot = torch.zeros(len(labels), n_classes)\\n    labels_onehot.scatter_(1, torch.tensor(labels).unsqueeze(1), 1)\\n    \\n    brier = torch.mean((probs - labels_onehot) ** 2).item()\\n    return brier\\n\\ndef bootstrap_ci(metric_func, probs, labels, n_bootstrap=1000, confidence=0.95):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Compute bootstrap confidence interval for a metric.\\n    \\n    Args:\\n        metric_func: Function that computes metric\\n        probs: Predicted probabilities\\n        labels: True labels\\n        n_bootstrap: Number of bootstrap samples\\n        confidence: Confidence level\\n    \\n    Returns:\\n        (mean, lower_ci, upper_ci)\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    probs_np = probs.numpy()\\n    labels_np = np.array(labels)\\n    n = len(labels_np)\\n    \\n    bootstrap_metrics = []\\n    for _ in range(n_bootstrap):\\n        indices = np.random.choice(n, size=n, replace=True)\\n        boot_probs = probs_np[indices]\\n        boot_labels = labels_np[indices]\\n        metric = metric_func(torch.tensor(boot_probs), boot_labels)\\n        bootstrap_metrics.append(metric)\\n    \\n    bootstrap_metrics = np.array(bootstrap_metrics)\\n    mean = np.mean(bootstrap_metrics)\\n    lower = np.percentile(bootstrap_metrics, (1 - confidence) / 2 * 100)\\n    upper = np.percentile(bootstrap_metrics, (1 + confidence) / 2 * 100)\\n    \\n    return mean, lower, upper\\n```\\n\\n### Main Experiment Loop\\n```python\\ndef run_experiment(dataset_name, logits, labels, n_classes):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Run full experiment for one dataset.\\n    \\n    Args:\\n        dataset_name: Name of dataset\\n        logits: Extracted logits (N, C)\\n        labels: True labels (N,)\\n        n_classes: Number of classes\\n    \\n    Returns:\\n        Dictionary of results\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    # Split data\\n    n = len(labels)\\n    indices = np.random.permutation(n)\\n    train_idx = indices[:int(0.6 * n)]\\n    val_idx = indices[int(0.6 * n):int(0.8 * n)]\\n    test_idx = indices[int(0.8 * n):]\\n    \\n    # Prepare splits\\n    train_logits = [logits[i] for i in train_idx]\\n    train_labels = [labels[i] for i in train_idx]\\n    val_logits = [logits[i] for i in val_idx]\\n    val_labels = [labels[i] for i in val_idx]\\n    test_logits = [logits[i] for i in test_idx]\\n    test_labels = [labels[i] for i in test_idx]\\n    \\n    results = {'dataset': dataset_name}\\n    \\n    # Method 1: Uncalibrated\\n    print(f\\\"\\\\n=== {dataset_name}: Uncalibrated ===\\\")\\n    test_probs = torch.softmax(torch.tensor(test_logits), dim=-1)\\n    test_preds = torch.argmax(test_probs, dim=-1)\\n    \\n    ece = compute_ece(test_probs, test_labels)\\n    brier = compute_brier_score(test_probs, test_labels, n_classes)\\n    nll = compute_nll(test_probs, test_labels)\\n    acc = (test_preds == torch.tensor(test_labels)).float().mean().item()\\n    \\n    ece_ci = bootstrap_ci(compute_ece, test_probs, test_labels)\\n    \\n    results['uncalibrated'] = {\\n        'ece': ece,\\n        'ece_ci': ece_ci,\\n        'brier': brier,\\n        'nll': nll,\\n        'accuracy': acc\\n    }\\n    \\n    # Method 2: Temperature Scaling\\n    print(f\\\"\\\\n=== {dataset_name}: Temperature Scaling ===\\\")\\n    T_opt, val_preds, val_confs, val_probs = temperature_scaling(\\n        val_logits, val_labels, val_logits, val_labels\\n    )\\n    \\n    # Apply optimal T to test set\\n    test_scaled = torch.tensor(test_logits) / T_opt\\n    test_probs_ts = torch.softmax(test_scaled, dim=-1)\\n    test_preds_ts = torch.argmax(test_probs_ts, dim=-1)\\n    \\n    ece_ts = compute_ece(test_probs_ts, test_labels)\\n    brier_ts = compute_brier_score(test_probs_ts, test_labels, n_classes)\\n    nll_ts = compute_nll(test_probs_ts, test_labels)\\n    acc_ts = (test_preds_ts == torch.tensor(test_labels)).float().mean().item()\\n    \\n    ece_ci_ts = bootstrap_ci(compute_ece, test_probs_ts, test_labels)\\n    \\n    results['temperature_scaling'] = {\\n        'T_optimal': T_opt,\\n        'ece': ece_ts,\\n        'ece_ci': ece_ci_ts,\\n        'brier': brier_ts,\\n        'nll': nll_ts,\\n        'accuracy': acc_ts\\n    }\\n    \\n    # Method 3: TEC\\n    print(f\\\"\\\\n=== {dataset_name}: TEC ===\\\")\\n    best_params, best_ece_val = tune_tec_hyperparameters(val_logits, val_labels)\\n    T_0_opt, alpha_opt, beta_opt = best_params\\n    \\n    # Apply optimal TEC to test set\\n    test_probs_tec, test_T_sample = tec_calibration(\\n        test_logits, T_0_opt, alpha_opt, beta_opt\\n    )\\n    test_preds_tec = torch.argmax(test_probs_tec, dim=-1)\\n    \\n    ece_tec = compute_ece(test_probs_tec, test_labels)\\n    brier_tec = compute_brier_score(test_probs_tec, test_labels, n_classes)\\n    nll_tec = compute_nll(test_probs_tec, test_labels)\\n    acc_tec = (test_preds_tec == torch.tensor(test_labels)).float().mean().item()\\n    \\n    ece_ci_tec = bootstrap_ci(compute_ece, test_probs_tec, test_labels)\\n    \\n    results['tec'] = {\\n        'T_0_optimal': T_0_opt,\\n        'alpha_optimal': alpha_opt,\\n        'beta_optimal': beta_opt,\\n        'ece': ece_tec,\\n        'ece_ci': ece_ci_tec,\\n        'brier': brier_tec,\\n        'nll': nll_tec,\\n        'accuracy': acc_tec\\n    }\\n    \\n    # Heterogeneous Split Analysis\\n    print(f\\\"\\\\n=== {dataset_name}: Heterogeneous Split Analysis ===\\\")\\n    easy_idx, hard_idx = create_heterogeneous_splits(test_logits, test_labels)\\n    \\n    for split_name, split_idx in [('easy', easy_idx), ('hard', hard_idx)]:\\n        split_logits = [test_logits[i] for i in split_idx]\\n        split_labels = [test_labels[i] for i in split_idx]\\n        \\n        # Uncalibrated\\n        split_probs = torch.softmax(torch.tensor(split_logits), dim=-1)\\n        ece_split = compute_ece(split_probs, split_labels)\\n        \\n        # TS\\n        split_scaled = torch.tensor(split_logits) / T_opt\\n        split_probs_ts = torch.softmax(split_scaled, dim=-1)\\n        ece_ts_split = compute_ece(split_probs_ts, split_labels)\\n        \\n        # TEC\\n        split_probs_tec, _ = tec_calibration(\\n            split_logits, T_0_opt, alpha_opt, beta_opt\\n        )\\n        ece_tec_split = compute_ece(split_probs_tec, split_labels)\\n        \\n        results[f'heterogeneous_{split_name}'] = {\\n            'n_samples': len(split_idx),\\n            'uncalibrated_ece': ece_split,\\n            'ts_ece': ece_ts_split,\\n            'tec_ece': ece_tec_split\\n        }\\n    \\n    return results\\n```\\n\\n### Output Format\\n```python\\ndef save_results(all_results, filename='method_out.json'):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Save results to method_out.json.\\n    \\n    Format:\\n    {\\n        \\\"experiment\\\": \\\"TEC_vs_TS_evaluation\\\",\\n        \\\"datasets\\\": [\\n            {\\n                \\\"dataset\\\": \\\"sst-2\\\",\\n                \\\"n_classes\\\": 2,\\n                \\\"results\\\": {\\n                    \\\"uncalibrated\\\": {...},\\n                    \\\"temperature_scaling\\\": {...},\\n                    \\\"tec\\\": {...},\\n                    \\\"heterogeneous_easy\\\": {...},\\n                    \\\"heterogeneous_hard\\\": {...}\\n                }\\n            },\\n            ...\\n        ],\\n        \\\"summary\\\": {\\n            \\\"teec_better_than_ts_count\\\": 2,\\n            \\\"ts_better_than_teec_count\\\": 3,\\n            \\\"average_ece_improvement_ts\\\": 0.05,\\n            \\\"average_ece_improvement_tec\\\": 0.03\\n        }\\n    }\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    with open(filename, 'w') as f:\\n        json.dump(all_results, f, indent=2)\\n```\",\n  \"fallback_plan\": \"## Fallback Plan\\n\\n### Issue 1: Pre-trained Models Not Available/Fail to Load\\n**Symptoms:** Unable to load HuggingFace models, model download fails, out of memory.\\n\\n**Fallback:**\\n1. Document as \\\"pilot study\\\" and note limitations\",\n  \"testing_plan\": \"## Testing Plan\\n\\n### Phase 1: Quick Sanity Check (15 minutes)\\n**Goal:** Verify data loading and model access Normalize entropy and margin to [0, 1]\\n    max_entropy = torch.log(torch.tensor(probs.shape[-1]).float())\\n    norm_entropy = entropy / max_entropy\\n    norm_margin = margin  # Already in [0, 1]\\n    \\n    # Compute per-sample temperature\\n    T_sample = T_0 * (1 + alpha * norm_entropy - beta * norm_margin)\\n    T_sample = torch.clamp(T_sample, min=0.01, max=100.0)  # Prevent extremes\\n    \\n    # Apply temperature scaling per sample\\n    # Need to handle per-sample temperature\\n    scaled_logits = torch.tensor(logits) / T_sample.unsqueeze(-1)\\n    calibrated_probs = torch.softmax(scaled_logits, dim=-1)\\n    \\n    return calibrated_probs, T_sample\\n\\ndef tune_tec_hyperparameters(val_logits, val_labels):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Grid search for TEC hyperparameters.\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    best_ece = float('inf')\\n    best_params = None\\n    \\n    T_0_range = [0.1, 0.5, 1.0, 2.0, 5.0, 10.0, 20.0]\\n    alpha_range = [0.0, 0.5, 1.0, 1.5, 2.0]\\n    beta_range = [0.0, 0.25, 0.5, 0.75, 1.0]\\n    \\n    for T_0 in T_0_range:\\n        for alpha in alpha_range:\\n            for beta in beta_range:\\n                probs, _ = tec_calibration(val_logits, T_0, alpha, beta)\\n                ece = compute_ece(probs, val_labels)\\n                \\n                if ece < best_ece:\\n                    best_ece = ece\\n                    best_params = (T_0, alpha, beta)\\n    \\n    return best_params, best_ece\\n```\\n\\n### Heterogeneous Split Creation\\n```python\\ndef create_heterogeneous_splits(logits, labels, easy_ratio=0.5):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Split dataset into easy (high margin) and hard (low margin) examples.\\n    \\n    Args:\\n        logits: Raw logits\\n        labels: True labels\\n        easy_ratio: Ratio of easy examples to include\\n    \\n    Returns:\\n        easy_indices, hard_indices\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    probs = torch.softmax(torch.tensor(logits), dim=-1)\\n    margin = compute_margin(probs)\\n    \\n    # Sort by margin\\n    sorted_indices = torch.argsort(margin, descending=True)\\n    \\n    n_easy = int(len(sorted_indices) * easy_ratio)\\n    easy_indices = sorted_indices[:n_easy]\\n    hard_indices = sorted_indices[n_easy:]\\n    \\n    return easy_indices, hard_indices\\n```\\n\\n### Metrics Computation\\n```python\\nimport numpy as np\\nfrom sklearn.metrics import brier_score_loss\\n\\ndef compute_ece(probs, labels, n_bins=10):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Compute Expected Calibration Error.\\n    \\n    Args:\\n        probs: Predicted probabilities (N, C)\\n        labels: True labels (N,)\\n        n_bins: Number of bins for calibration\\n    \\n    Returns:\\n        ECE value\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    # Softmax without temperature scaling\\n    probs = torch.softmax(torch.tensor(logits), dim=-1)\\n    preds = torch.argmax(probs, dim=-1)\\n    confs = torch.max(probs, dim=-1).values\\n    return preds, confs, probs\\n```\\n\\n### Method2: Temperature Scaling (TS)\\n```python\\nimport torch.nn as nn\\nimport torch.optim as optim\\n\\ndef temperature_scaling(logits, labels, val_logits, val_labels):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Tune temperature T on validation set to minimize NLL.\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    # Initialize temperature\\n    temperature = nn.Parameter(torch.ones(1) * 1.0)\\n    optimizer = optim.LBFGS([temperature], lr=0.01, max_iter=50)\\n    \\n    logits_tensor = torch.tensor(logits)\\n    labels_tensor = torch.tensor(labels)\\n    \\n    def eval():\\n        optimizer.zero_grad()\\n        scaled_logits = logits_tensor / temperature\\n        loss = nn.CrossEntropyLoss()(scaled_logits, labels_tensor)\\n        loss.backward()\\n        return loss\\n    \\n    # Optimize temperature\\n    for _ in range(100):\\n        optimizer.step(eval)\\n    \\n    # Apply to validation set\\n    with torch.no_grad():\\n        val_scaled = torch.tensor(val_logits) / temperature\\n        val_probs = torch.softmax(val_scaled, dim=-1)\\n        val_preds = torch.argmax(val_probs, dim=-1)\\n        val_confs = torch.max(val_probs, dim=-1).values\\n    \\n    return temperature.item(), val_preds, val_confs, val_probs\\n```\\n\\n### Method3: Thermodynamic Entropy Calibration (TEC)\\n```python\\ndef compute_entropy(probs):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Compute Shannon entropy of probability distribution.\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    epsilon = 1e-12\\n    probs = torch.clamp(probs, epsilon, 1.0 - epsilon)\\n    entropy = -torch.sum(probs * torch.log(probs), dim=-1)\\n    return entropy\\n\\ndef compute_margin(probs):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Compute decision margin (difference between top-2 predictions).\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    sorted_probs, _ = torch.sort(probs, dim=-1, descending=True)\\n    margin = sorted_probs[..., 0] - sorted_probs[..., 1]\\n    return margin\\n\\ndef tec_calibration(logits, T_0, alpha, beta):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Thermodynamic Entropy Calibration.\\n    \\n    Adjusts per-sample temperature based on entropy and margin:\\n    T_sample = T_0 * (1 + alpha * entropy - beta * margin)\\n    \\n    Args:\\n        logits: Raw logits (N, C)\\n        T_0: Base temperature parameter\\n        alpha: Entropy weight parameter\\n        beta: Margin weight parameter\\n    \\n    Returns:\\n        Calibrated probabilities\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    probs = torch.softmax(torch.tensor(logits), dim=-1)\\n    entropy = compute_entropy(probs)\\n    margin = compute_margin(probs)\\n    \\n    # Normalize entropy and margin to [0, 1]\\n    max_entropy = torch.log(torch.tensor(probs.shape[-1]).float())\\n    norm_entropy = entropy / max_entropy\\n    norm_margin = margin  # Already in [0, 1]\\n    \\n    # Compute per-sample temperature\\n    T_sample = T_0 * (1 + alpha * norm_entropy - beta * norm_margin)\\n    T_sample = torch.clamp(T_sample, min=0.01, max=100.0)  # Prevent extremes\\n    \\n    # Apply temperature scaling per sample\\n    # Need to handle per-sample temperature\\n    scaled_logits = torch.tensor(logits) / T_sample.unsqueeze(-1)\\n    calibrated_probs = torch.softmax(scaled_logits, dim=-1)\\n    \\n    return calibrated_probs, T_sample\\n\\ndef tune_tec_hyperparameters(val_logits, val_labels):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Grid search for TEC hyperparameters.\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    best_ece = float('inf')\\n    best_params = None\\n    \\n    T_0_range = [0.1, 0.5, 1.0, 2.0, 5.0, 10.0, 20.0]\\n    alpha_range = [0.0, 0.5, 1.0, 1.5, 2.0]\\n    beta_range = [0.0, 0.25, 0.5, 0.75, 1.0]\\n    \\n    for T_0 in T_0_range:\\n        for alpha in alpha_range:\\n            for beta in beta_range:\\n                probs, _ = tec_calibration(val_logits, T_0, alpha, beta)\\n                ece = compute_ece(probs, val_labels)\\n                \\n                if ece < best_ece:\\n                    best_ece = ece\\n                    best_params = (T_0, alpha, beta)\\n    \\n    return best_params, best_ece\\n```\\n\\n### Heterogeneous Split Creation\\n```python\\ndef create_heterogeneous_splits(logits, labels, easy_ratio=0.5):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Split dataset into easy (high margin) and hard (low margin) examples.\\n    \\n    Args:\\n        logits: Raw logits\\n        labels: True labels\\n        easy_ratio: Ratio of easy examples to include\\n    \\n    Returns:\\n        easy_indices, hard_indices\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    probs = torch.softmax(torch.tensor(logits), dim=-1)\\n    margin = compute_margin(probs)\\n    \\n    # Sort by margin\\n    sorted_indices = torch.argsort(margin, descending=True)\\n    \\n    n_easy = int(len(sorted_indices) * easy_ratio)\\n    easy_indices = sorted_indices[:n_easy]\\n    hard_indices = sorted_indices[n_easy:]\\n    \\n    return easy_indices, hard_indices\\n```\\n\\n### Metrics Computation\\n```python\\nimport numpy as np\\nfrom sklearn.metrics import brier_score_loss\\n\\ndef compute_ece(probs, labels, n_bins=10):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Compute Expected Calibration Error.\\n    \\n    Args:\\n        probs: Predicted probabilities (N, C)\\n        labels: True labels (N,)\\n        n_bins: Number of bins for calibration\\n    \\n    Returns:\\n        ECE value\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    # Get confidence and predictions\\n    confs = torch.max(probs, dim=-1).values.numpy()\\n    preds = torch.argmax(probs, dim=-1).numpy()\\n    labels = np.array(labels)\\n    \\n    # Bin predictions\\n    bins = np.linspace(0, 1, n_bins + 1)\\n    ece = 0.0\\n    \\n    for i in range(n_bins):\\n        mask = (confs >= bins[i]) & (confs < bins[i + 1])\\n        if mask.sum() > 0:\\n            bin_acc = np.mean(preds[mask] == labels[mask])\\n            bin_conf = np.mean(confs[mask])\\n            ece += np.abs(bin_acc - bin_conf) * mask.sum() / len(confs)\\n    \\n    return ece\\n\\ndef compute_nll(probs, labels):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Compute Negative Log-Likelihood.\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    probs = torch.clamp(probs, min=1e-12, max=1.0)\\n    labels = torch.tensor(labels)\\n    nll = -torch.log(probs[torch.arange(len(labels)), labels]).mean()\\n    return nll.item()\\n\\ndef compute_brier_score(probs, labels, n_classes):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Compute Brier Score.\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    # One-hot encode labels\\n    labels_onehot = torch.zeros(len(labels), n_classes)\\n    labels_onehot.scatter_(1, torch.tensor(labels).unsqueeze(1), 1)\\n    \\n    brier = torch.mean((probs - labels_onehot) ** 2).item()\\n    return brier\\n\\ndef bootstrap_ci(metric_func, probs, labels, n_bootstrap=1000, confidence=0.95):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Compute bootstrap confidence interval for a metric.\\n    \\n    Args:\\n        metric_func: Function that computes metric\\n        probs: Predicted probabilities\\n        labels: True labels\\n        n_bootstrap: Number of bootstrap samples\\n        confidence: Confidence level\\n    \\n    Returns:\\n        (mean, lower_ci, upper_ci)\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    probs_np = probs.numpy()\\n    labels_np = np.array(labels)\\n    n = len(labels_np)\\n    \\n    bootstrap_metrics = []\\n    for _ in range(n_bootstrap):\\n        indices = np.random.choice(n, size=n, replace=True)\\n        boot_probs = probs_np[indices]\\n        boot_labels = labels_np[indices]\\n        metric = metric_func(torch.tensor(boot_probs), boot_labels)\\n        bootstrap_metrics.append(metric)\\n    \\n    bootstrap_metrics = np.array(bootstrap_metrics)\\n    mean = np.mean(bootstrap_metrics)\\n    lower = np.percentile(bootstrap_metrics, (1 - confidence) / 2 * 100)\\n    upper = np.percentile(bootstrap_metrics, (1 + confidence) / 2 * 100)\\n    \\n    return mean, lower, upper\\n```\\n\\n### Main Experiment Loop\\n```python\\ndef run_experiment(dataset_name, logits, labels, n_classes):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Run full experiment for one dataset.\\n    \\n    Args:\\n        dataset_name: Name of dataset\\n        logits: Extracted logits (N, C)\\n        labels: True labels (N,)\\n        n_classes: Number of classes\\n    \\n    Returns:\\n        Dictionary of results\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    # Split data\\n    n = len(labels)\\n    indices = np.random.permutation(n)\\n    train_idx = indices[:int(0.6 * n)]\\n    val_idx = indices[int(0.6 * n):int(0.8 * n)]\\n    test_idx = indices[int(0.8 * n):]\\n    \\n    # Prepare splits\\n    train_logits = [logits[i] for i in train_idx]\\n    train_labels = [labels[i] for i in train_idx]\\n    val_logits = [logits[i] for i in val_idx]\\n    val_labels = [labels[i] for i in val_idx]\\n    test_logits = [logits[i] for i in test_idx]\\n    test_labels = [labels[i] for i in test_idx]\\n    \\n    results = {'dataset': dataset_name}\\n    \\n    # Method 1: Uncalibrated\\n    print(f\\\"\\\\n=== {dataset_name}: Uncalibrated ===\\\")\\n    test_probs = torch.softmax(torch.tensor(test_logits), dim=-1)\\n    test_preds = torch.argmax(test_probs, dim=-1)\\n    \\n    ece = compute_ece(test_probs, test_labels)\\n    brier = compute_brier_score(test_probs, test_labels, n_classes)\\n    nll = compute_nll(test_probs, test_labels)\\n    acc = (test_preds == torch.tensor(test_labels)).float().mean().item()\\n    \\n    ece_ci = bootstrap_ci(compute_ece, test_probs, test_labels)\\n    \\n    results['uncalibrated'] = {\\n        'ece': ece,\\n        'ece_ci': ece_ci,\\n        'brier': brier,\\n        'nll': nll,\\n        'accuracy': acc\\n    }\\n    \\n    # Method 2: Temperature Scaling\\n    print(f\\\"\\\\n=== {dataset_name}: Temperature Scaling ===\\\")\\n    T_opt, val_preds, val_confs, val_probs = temperature_scaling(\\n        val_logits, val_labels, val_logits, val_labels\\n    )\\n    \\n    # Apply optimal T to test set\\n    test_scaled = torch.tensor(test_logits) / T_opt\\n    test_probs_ts = torch.softmax(test_scaled, dim=-1)\\n    test_preds_ts = torch.argmax(test_probs_ts, dim=-1)\\n    \\n    ece_ts = compute_ece(test_probs_ts, test_labels)\\n    brier_ts = compute_brier_score(test_probs_ts, test_labels, n_classes)\\n    nll_ts = compute_nll(test_probs_ts, test_labels)\\n    acc_ts = (test_preds_ts == torch.tensor(test_labels)).float().mean().item()\\n    \\n    ece_ci_ts = bootstrap_ci(compute_ece, test_probs_ts, test_labels)\\n    \\n    results['temperature_scaling'] = {\\n        'T_optimal': T_opt,\\n        'ece': ece_ts,\\n        'ece_ci': ece_ci_ts,\\n        'brier': brier_ts,\\n        'nll': nll_ts,\\n        'accuracy': acc_ts\\n    }\\n    \\n    # Method 3: TEC\\n    print(f\\\"\\\\n=== {dataset_name}: TEC ===\\\")\\n    best_params, best_ece_val = tune_tec_hyperparameters(val_logits, val_labels)\\n    T_0_opt, alpha_opt, beta_opt = best_params\\n    \\n    # Apply optimal TEC to test set\\n    test_probs_tec, test_T_sample = tec_calibration(\\n        test_logits, T_0_opt, alpha_opt, beta_opt\\n    )\\n    test_preds_tec = torch.argmax(test_probs_tec, dim=-1)\\n    \\n    ece_tec = compute_ece(test_probs_tec, test_labels)\\n    brier_tec = compute_brier_score(test_probs_tec, test_labels, n_classes)\\n    nll_tec = compute_nll(test_probs_tec, test_labels)\\n    acc_tec = (test_preds_tec == torch.tensor(test_labels)).float().mean().item()\\n    \\n    ece_ci_tec = bootstrap_ci(compute_ece, test_probs_tec, test_labels)\\n    \\n    results['tec'] = {\\n        'T_0_optimal': T_0_opt,\\n        'alpha_optimal': alpha_opt,\\n        'beta_optimal': beta_opt,\\n        'ece': ece_tec,\\n        'ece_ci': ece_ci_tec,\\n        'brier': brier_tec,\\n        'nll': nll_tec,\\n        'accuracy': acc_tec\\n    }\\n    \\n    # Heterogeneous Split Analysis\\n    print(f\\\"\\\\n=== {dataset_name}: Heterogeneous Split Analysis ===\\\")\\n    easy_idx, hard_idx = create_heterogeneous_splits(test_logits, test_labels)\\n    \\n    for split_name, split_idx in [('easy', easy_idx), ('hard', hard_idx)]:\\n        split_logits = [test_logits[i] for i in split_idx]\\n        split_labels = [test_labels[i] for i in split_idx]\\n        \\n        # Uncalibrated\\n        split_probs = torch.softmax(torch.tensor(split_logits), dim=-1)\\n        ece_split = compute_ece(split_probs, split_labels)\\n        \\n        # TS\\n        split_scaled = torch.tensor(split_logits) / T_opt\\n        split_probs_ts = torch.softmax(split_scaled, dim=-1)\\n        ece_ts_split = compute_ece(split_probs_ts, split_labels)\\n        \\n        # TEC\\n        split_probs_tec, _ = tec_calibration(\\n            split_logits, T_0_opt, alpha_opt, beta_opt\\n        )\\n        ece_tec_split = compute_ece(split_probs_tec, split_labels)\\n        \\n        results[f'heterogeneous_{split_name}'] = {\\n            'n_samples': len(split_idx),\\n            'uncalibrated_ece': ece_split,\\n            'ts_ece': ece_ts_split,\\n            'tec_ece': ece_tec_split\\n        }\\n    \\n    return results\\n```\\n\\n### Output Format\\n```python\\ndef save_results(all_results, filename='method_out.json'):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Save results to method_out.json.\\n    \\n    Format:\\n    {\\n        \\\"experiment\\\": \\\"TEC_vs_TS_evaluation\\\",\\n        \\\"datasets\\\": [\\n            {\\n                \\\"dataset\\\": \\\"sst-2\\\",\\n                \\\"n_classes\\\": 2,\\n                \\\"results\\\": {\\n                    \\\"uncalibrated\\\": {...},\\n                    \\\"temperature_scaling\\\": {...},\\n                    \\\"tec\\\": {...},\\n                    \\\"heterogeneous_easy\\\": {...},\\n                    \\\"heterogeneous_hard\\\": {...}\\n                }\\n            },\\n            ...\\n        ],\\n        \\\"summary\\\": {\\n            \\\"teec_better_than_ts_count\\\": 2,\\n            \\\"ts_better_than_teec_count\\\": 3,\\n            \\\"average_ece_improvement_ts\\\": 0.05,\\n            \\\"average_ece_improvement_tec\\\": 0.03\\n        }\\n    }\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    with open(filename, 'w') as f:\\n        json.dump(all_results, f, indent=2)\\n```\",\n  \"fallback_plan\": \"## Fallback Plan\\n\\n### Issue 1: Pre-trained Models Not Available/Fail to Load\\n**Symptoms:** Unable to load HuggingFace models, model download fails, out of memory.\\n\\n**Fallback:**\\n1. Use smaller/distilled versions of models:\\n   - Use `distilbert-base-uncased` instead of BERT/RoBERTa\\n   - Use `bert-base-uncased` with minimal fine-tuning on each dataset\\n2. If still failing, use synthetic logits sampled from real distribution:\\n   - Fit a simple classifier (LogisticRegression) on each dataset\\n   - Extract decision function values as \\\"logits\\\"\\n   - Use these as approximation of LLM logits\\n\\n### Issue 2: TEC Hyperparameter Tuning Too Slow\\n**Symptoms:** Grid search takes too long, exceeds time budget.\\n\\n**Fallback:**\\n1. Reduce hyperparameter grid:\\n   - T_0: [0.5, 1.0, 2.0, 5.0]\\n   - alpha: [0.0, 1.0, 2.0]\\n   - beta: [0.0, 0.5, 1.0]\\n2. Use random search instead of grid search (sample 20 combinations)\\n3. Use validation ECE as objective (faster than cross-validation)\\n\\n### Issue 3: GPU Memory Insufficient for Large Models\\n**Symptoms:** OOM errors when loading models or processing data.\\n\\n**Fallback:**\\n1. Process data in smaller batches (batch_size=8 or 16)\\n2. Use CPU for inference (slower but works):\\n   ```python\\n   model.cpu()\\n   torch.set_num_threads(4)  # Use multiple CPU threads\\n   ```\\n3. Use gradient checkpointing or model quantization (8-bit)\\n\\n### Issue 4: Bootstrap CI Computation Too Slow\\n**Symptoms:** 1000 bootstrap samples take too long.\\n\\n**Fallback:**\\n1. Reduce to 100 bootstrap samples\\n2. Use analytical CI approximation if distribution is approximately normal\\n3. Compute only ECE and skip CI if time is critical\\n\\n### Issue 5: TEC Implementation Unclear or Fails\\n**Symptoms:** TEC formula unclear from hypothesis, implementation produces NaNs or poor results.\\n\\n**Fallback:**\\n1. Simplify TEC to basic form:\\n   - Use only entropy-based adjustment: `T = T_0 * (1 + alpha * entropy)`\\n   - Or only margin-based: `T = T_0 * (1 - beta * margin)`\\n2. Compare multiple TEC variants:\\n   - TEC-entropy (entropy only)\\n   - TEC-margin (margin only)\\n   - TEC-full (both)\\n3. If all fail, treat as ablation study: \\\"TEC variants fail to outperform TS\\\"\\n\\n### Issue 6: Datasets Too Large to Process\\n**Symptoms:** Processing all 150K examples exceeds time budget.\\n\\n**Fallback:**\\n1. Use subset of data:\\n   - Sample 10K examples per dataset (stratified by class)\\n   - Ensure validation set has at least 1K examples for tuning\\n2. Process only 3 datasets instead of 5:\\n   - Prioritize: SST-2 (binary), MNLI (3-class), DBpedia (14-class)\\n   - Covers binary, few-class, many-class scenarios\\n\\n### Issue 7: Metrics Computation Errors\\n**Symptoms:** ECE computation produces unreasonable values, Brier score formula incorrect.\\n\\n**Fallback:**\\n1. Use standard library implementations:\\n   - Use `sklearn.calibration.calibration_curve` for ECE\\n   - Verify Brier score with `sklearn.metrics.brier_score_loss` (for binary)\\n   - For multi-class, implement as MSE between probs and one-hot labels\\n2. Test metrics on simple cases first:\\n   - Perfect calibration: probs = accuracies in each bin\\n   - Random predictions: ECE should be high\\n3. Visualize reliability diagrams to verify ECE computation\\n\\n### Minimum Viable Experiment (if all else fails)\\nIf multiple issues compound and time is running out:\\n1. Run only on SST-2 dataset (smallest, simplest)\\n2. Compare only Uncalibrated vs Temperature Scaling (skip TEC)\\n3. Compute only ECE and accuracy (skip Brier, NLL, bootstrap CI)\\n4. Use 1K examples for fast iteration\\n5. Document as \\\"pilot study\\\" and note limitations\",\n  \"testing_plan\": \"## Testing Plan\\n\\n### Phase1: Quick Sanity Check (15 minutes)\\n**Goal:** Verify data loading and model access work.\\n\\n```python\\n# Test 1: Load dependency dataset\\nimport json\\nwith open('../iter_1/gen_art/gen_art_dataset_1/full_data_out.json', 'r') as f:\\n    data = json.load(f)\\nprint(f\\\"Loaded {data['metadata']['total_examples']} examples\\\")\\nprint(f\\\"Datasets: {[d['dataset'] for d in data['datasets']]}\\\")\\n\\n# Test 2: Load one pre-trained model\\nfrom transformers import AutoModelForSequenceClassification, AutoTokenizer\\nmodel_name = 'distilbert-base-uncased-finetuned-sst-2-english'\\ntry:\\n    tokenizer = AutoTokenizer.from_pretrained(model_name)\\n    model = AutoModelForSequenceClassification.from_pretrained(model_name)\\n    print(f\\\"Model loaded: {model_name}\\\")\\n    print(f\\\"Model output shape: {model.config.num_labels} classes\\\")\\nexcept Exception as e:\\n    print(f\\\"Model loading failed: {e}\\\")\\n    print(\\\"Will use fallback plan\\\")\\n\\n# Test 3: Extract logits for 10 examples\\nimport torch\\nsample_examples = data['datasets'][0]['examples'][:10]\\nwith torch.no_grad():\\n    for ex in sample_examples:\\n        inputs = tokenizer(ex['input'], return_tensors='pt', truncation=True)\\n        outputs = model(**inputs)\\n        logits = outputs.logits\\n        print(f\\\"Logits shape: {logits.shape}, Label: {ex['output']}\\\")\\n        break  # Just test one\\nprint(\\\"Logit extraction works!\\\")\\n```\\n\\n### Phase 2: Method Implementation Verification (30 minutes)\\n**Goal:** Verify each method computes reasonable outputs.\\n\\n```python\\n# Test 1: Uncalibrated baseline\\nlogits = torch.randn(100, 2)  # Simulate 100 examples, 2 classes\\nprobs = torch.softmax(logits, dim=-1)\\npreds = torch.argmax(probs, dim=-1)\\nprint(f\\\"Uncalibrated: preds shape {preds.shape}, probs range [{probs.min():.3f}, {probs.max():.3f}]\\\")\\n\\n# Test 2: Temperature scaling\\nfrom torch import nn, optim\\nT = nn.Parameter(torch.ones(1))\\nprint(f\\\"Initial T: {T.item()}\\\")\\n# Simulate optimization step\\nscaled_logits = logits / T\\nloss = nn.CrossEntropyLoss()(scaled_logits, preds)\\nprint(f\\\"TS loss: {loss.item():.3f}\\\")\\n\\n# Test 3: TEC calibration\\n# Simulate TEC with dummy parameters\\nalpha, beta, T_0 = 1.0, 0.5, 1.0\\nentropy = -torch.sum(probs * torch.log(probs + 1e-12), dim=-1)\\nmargin = torch.sort(probs, dim=-1, descending=True).values\\nmargin = margin[:, 0] - margin[:, 1]\\nT_sample = T_0 * (1 + alpha * entropy - beta * margin)\\nprint(f\\\"TEC: T_sample range [{T_sample.min():.3f}, {T_sample.max():.3f}]\\\")\\n```\\n\\n### Phase 3: Metrics Computation Verification (20 minutes)\\n**Goal:** Verify metrics are computed correctly.\\n\\n```python\\n# Test ECE computation\\nimport numpy as np\\n\\ndef test_ece():\\n    # Case 1: Perfect calibration\\n    n = 1000\\n    probs = torch.linspace(0.1, 0.9, n)\\n    # If confidence = accuracy, ECE should be 0\\n    labels = (torch.rand(n) < probs).long()  # Probabilistic labels\\n    \\n    ece = compute_ece(probs.unsqueeze(-1).expand(-1, 2), labels)\\n    print(f\\\"Perfect calibration ECE: {ece:.4f} (should be near 0)\\\")\\n    \\n    # Case 2: Overconfident predictions\\n    probs_overconf = torch.ones(n) * 0.9\\n    labels_random = torch.randint(0, 2, (n,))\\n    ece_overconf = compute_ece(probs_overconf.unsqueeze(-1).expand(-1, 2), labels_random)\\n    print(f\\\"Overconfident ECE: {ece_overconf:.4f} (should be high)\\\")\\n\\ntest_ece()\\n\\n# Test Brier score\\nfrom sklearn.metrics import brier_score_loss\\ny_true = [0, 1, 0, 1]\\ny_prob = [0.1, 0.9, 0.2, 0.8]\\nbrier = brier_score_loss(y_true, y_prob)\\nprint(f\\\"Brier score (binary): {brier:.4f}\\\")\\nprint(f\\\"Expected: {(0.1**2 + 0.1**2 + 0.2**2 + 0.2**2) / 4:.4f}\\\")\\n```\\n\\n### Phase 4: Small-Scale Experiment (1 hour)\\n**Goal:** Run full pipeline on mini dataset (15 examples) to verify end-to-end.\\n\\n```python\\n# Use mini_data_out.json (15 examples)\\nwith open('../iter_1/gen_art/gen_art_dataset_1/mini_data_out.json', 'r') as f:\\n    mini_data = json.load(f)\\n\\n# Run on 1 dataset with 15 examples\\nfor dataset in mini_data['datasets'][:1]:  # Just SST-2\\n    print(f\\\"\\\\nTesting on {dataset['dataset']} with {len(dataset['examples'])} examples\\\")\\n    \\n    # Extract logits\\n    logits = []\\n    labels = []\\n    for ex in dataset['examples']:\\n        inputs = tokenizer(ex['input'], return_tensors='pt', truncation=True, padding=True)\\n        with torch.no_grad():\\n            outputs = model(**inputs)\\n            logits.append(outputs.logits.squeeze(0).numpy().tolist())\\n            labels.append(int(ex['output']))\\n    \\n    # Run methods\\n    results = run_experiment(\\n        dataset['dataset'],\\n        logits,\\n        labels,\\n        n_classes=2\\n    )\\n    \\n    print(f\\\"Results:\\\")\\n    print(f\\\"  Uncalibrated ECE: {results['uncalibrated']['ece']:.4f}\\\")\\n    print(f\\\"  TS ECE: {results['temperature_scaling']['ece']:.4f}\\\")\\n    print(f\\\"  TEC ECE: {results['tec']['ece']:.4f}\\\")\\n```\\n\\n### Phase 5: Medium-Scale Experiment (2 hours)\\n**Goal:** Run on 1 dataset with 1K examples to verify scalability.\\n\\n```python\\n# Sample 1K examples from full dataset\\nimport random\\nrandom.seed(42)\\n\\nwith open('../iter_1/gen_art/gen_art_dataset_1/full_data_out.json', 'r') as f:\\n    full_data = json.load(f)\\n\\nsst2_data = full_data['datasets'][0]\\nsampled_examples = random.sample(sst2_data['examples'], 1000)\\n\\n# Extract logits (batch processing for speed)\\nlogits = []\\nlabels = []\\nmodel.eval()\\n\\nbatch_size = 32\\nfor i in range(0, len(sampled_examples), batch_size):\\n    batch = sampled_examples[i:i+batch_size]\\n    texts = [ex['input'] for ex in batch]\\n    \\n    inputs = tokenizer(texts, return_tensors='pt', truncation=True, padding=True)\\n    with torch.no_grad():\\n        outputs = model(**inputs)\\n        batch_logits = outputs.logits.numpy()\\n Evaluate on heterogeneous splits with bootstrap CI.\",\n  \"runpod_compute_profile\": \"gpu\",\n  \"implementation_pseudocode\": \"## Experimental Setup\\n\\n### Dataset Preparation\\n1. Load the standardized datasets from the dependency artifact (full_data_out.json)\\n2. For each dataset, load the appropriate pre-trained model:\\n   - SST-2: distilbert-base-uncased-finetuned-sst-2-english\\n   - QNLI: distilbert-base-uncased-finetuned-sst-2-english (or BERT-base)\\n   - AG News: roberta-base (fine-tuned on AG News)\\n   - MNLI: roberta-large-mnli (or roberta-base)\\n   - DBpedia: bert-base-uncased (fine-tuned on DBpedia)\\n3. Split each dataset into:\\n   - Train (60%): for model fine-tuning if needed\\n   - Validation (20%): for hyperparameter tuning\\n   - Test (20%): for final evaluation\\n\\n### Model & Logit Extraction\\n```python\\nimport torch\\nfrom transformers import AutoModelForSequenceClassification, AutoTokenizer\\nfrom torch.utils.data import DataLoader\\nimport json\\n\\n# Load dataset\\nwith open('full_data_out.json', 'r') as f:\\n    data = json.load(f)\\n\\n# Model mapping\\ndataset_models = {\\n    'sst-2': 'distilbert-base-uncased-finetuned-sst-2-english',\\n    'qnli': 'bert-base-uncased',  # May need QNLI fine-tuned version\\n    'ag_news': 'roberta-base',  # May need AG News fine-tuned\\n    'mnli': 'roberta-large-mnli',\\n    'dbpedia': 'bert-base-uncased'  # May need DBpedia fine-tuned\\n}\\n\\n# Extract logits for each dataset\\nfor dataset_name, model_name in dataset_models.items():\\n    tokenizer = AutoTokenizer.from_pretrained(model_name)\\n    model = AutoModelForSequenceClassification.from_pretrained(model_name)\\n    model.eval()\\n    \\n    # Get dataset examples\\n    dataset = [d for d in data['datasets'] if d['dataset'] == dataset_name][0]\\n    examples = dataset['examples']\\n    \\n    # Extract logits (no gradient)\\n    with torch.no_grad():\\n        for ex in examples:\\n            inputs = tokenizer(ex['input'], return_tensors='pt', truncation=True, padding=True)\\n            outputs = model(**inputs)\\n            logits = outputs.logits\\n            # Store logits with example\\n            ex['logits'] = logits.numpy().tolist()\\n            ex['num_classes'] = logits.shape[-1]\\n```\\n\\n### Method1: Uncalibrated Baseline\\n```python\\ndef uncalibrated_predictions(logits):\\n    # Softmax without temperature scaling\\n    probs = torch.softmax(torch.tensor(logits), dim=-1)\\n    preds = torch.argmax(probs, dim=-1)\\n    confs = torch.max(probs, dim=-1).values\\n    return preds, confs, probs\\n```\\n\\n### Method2: Temperature Scaling (TS)\\n```python\\nimport torch.nn as nn\\nimport torch.optim as optim\\n\\ndef temperature_scaling(logits, labels, val_logits, val_labels):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Tune temperature T on validation set to minimize NLL.\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    # Initialize temperature\\n    temperature = nn.Parameter(torch.ones(1) * 1.0)\\n    optimizer = optim.LBFGS([temperature], lr=0.01, max_iter=50)\\n    \\n    logits_tensor = torch.tensor(logits)\\n    labels_tensor = torch.tensor(labels)\\n    \\n    def eval():\\n        optimizer.zero_grad()\\n        scaled_logits = logits_tensor / temperature\\n        loss = nn.CrossEntropyLoss()(scaled_logits, labels_tensor)\\n        loss.backward()\\n        return loss\\n    \\n    # Optimize temperature\\n    for _ in range(100):\\n        optimizer.step(eval)\\n    \\n    # Apply to validation set\\n    with torch.no_grad():\\n        val_scaled = torch.tensor(val_logits) / temperature\\n        val_probs = torch.softmax(val_scaled, dim=-1)\\n        val_preds = torch.argmax(val_probs, dim=-1)\\n        val_confs = torch.max(val_probs, dim=-1).values\\n    \\n    return temperature.item(), val_preds, val_confs, val_probs\\n```\\n\\n### Method3: Thermodynamic Entropy Calibration (TEC)\\n```python\\ndef compute_entropy(probs):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Compute Shannon entropy of probability distribution.\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    epsilon = 1e-12\\n    probs = torch.clamp(probs, epsilon, 1.0 - epsilon)\\n    entropy = -torch.sum(probs * torch.log(probs), dim=-1)\\n    return entropy\\n\\ndef compute_margin(probs):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Compute decision margin (difference between top-2 predictions).\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    sorted_probs, _ = torch.sort(probs, dim=-1, descending=True)\\n    margin = sorted_probs[..., 0] - sorted_probs[..., 1]\\n    return margin\\n\\ndef tec_calibration(logits, T_0, alpha, beta):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Thermodynamic Entropy Calibration.\\n    \\n    Adjusts per-sample temperature based on entropy and margin:\\n    T_sample = T_0 * (1 + alpha * entropy - beta * margin)\\n    \\n    Args:\\n        logits: Raw logits (N, C)\\n        T_0: Base temperature parameter\\n        alpha: Entropy weight parameter\\n        beta: Margin weight parameter\\n    \\n    Returns:\\n        Calibrated probabilities\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    probs = torch.softmax(torch.tensor(logits), dim=-1)\\n    entropy = compute_entropy(probs)\\n    margin = compute_margin(probs)\\n    \\n    # Normalize entropy and margin to [0, 1]\\n    max_entropy = torch.log(torch.tensor(probs.shape[-1]).float())\\n    norm_entropy = entropy / max_entropy\\n    norm_margin = margin  # Already in [0, 1]\\n    \\n    # Compute per-sample temperature\\n    T_sample = T_0 * (1 + alpha * norm_entropy - beta * norm_margin)\\n    T_sample = torch.clamp(T_sample, min=0.01, max=100.0)  # Prevent extremes\\n    \\n    # Apply temperature scaling per sample\\n    # Need to handle per-sample temperature\\n    scaled_logits = torch.tensor(logits) / T_sample.unsqueeze(-1)\\n    calibrated_probs = torch.softmax(scaled_logits, dim=-1)\\n    \\n    return calibrated_probs, T_sample\\n\\ndef tune_tec_hyperparameters(val_logits, val_labels):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Grid search for TEC hyperparameters.\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    best_ece = float('inf')\\n    best_params = None\\n    \\n    T_0_range = [0.1, 0.5, 1.0, 2.0, 5.0, 10.0, 20.0]\\n    alpha_range = [0.0, 0.5, 1.0, 1.5, 2.0]\\n    beta_range = [0.0, 0.25, 0.5, 0.75, 1.0]\\n    \\n    for T_0 in T_0_range:\\n        for alpha in alpha_range:\\n            for beta in beta_range:\\n                probs, _ = tec_calibration(val_logits, T_0, alpha, beta)\\n                ece = compute_ece(probs, val_labels)\\n                \\n                if ece < best_ece:\\n                    best_ece = ece\\n                    best_params = (T_0, alpha, beta)\\n    \\n    return best_params, best_ece\\n```\\n\\n### Heterogeneous Split Creation\\n```python\\ndef create_heterogeneous_splits(logits, labels, easy_ratio=0.5):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Split dataset into easy (high margin) and hard (low margin) examples.\\n    \\n    Args:\\n        logits: Raw logits\\n        labels: True labels\\n        easy_ratio: Ratio of easy examples to include\\n    \\n    Returns:\\n        easy_indices, hard_indices\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    probs = torch.softmax(torch.tensor(logits), dim=-1)\\n    margin = compute_margin(probs)\\n    \\n    # Sort by margin\\n    sorted_indices = torch.argsort(margin, descending=True)\\n    \\n    n_easy = int(len(sorted_indices) * easy_ratio)\\n    easy_indices = sorted_indices[:n_easy]\\n    hard_indices = sorted_indices[n_easy:]\\n    \\n    return easy_indices, hard_indices\\n```\\n\\n### Metrics Computation\\n```python\\nimport numpy as np\\nfrom sklearn.metrics import brier_score_loss\\n\\ndef compute_ece(probs, labels, n_bins=10):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Compute Expected Calibration Error.\\n    \\n    Args:\\n        probs: Predicted probabilities (N, C)\\n        labels: True labels (N,)\\n        n_bins: Number of bins for calibration\\n    \\n    Returns:\\n        ECE value\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    # Get confidence and predictions\\n    confs = torch.max(probs, dim=-1).values.numpy()\\n    preds = torch.argmax(probs, dim=-1).numpy()\\n    labels = np.array(labels)\\n    \\n    # Bin predictions\\n    bins = np.linspace(0, 1, n_bins + 1)\\n    ece = 0.0\\n    \\n    for i in range(n_bins):\\n        mask = (confs >= bins[i]) & (confs < bins[i + 1])\\n        if mask.sum() > 0:\\n            bin_acc = np.mean(preds[mask] == labels[mask])\\n            bin_conf = np.mean(confs[mask])\\n            ece += np.abs(bin_acc - bin_conf) * mask.sum() / len(confs)\\n    \\n    return ece\\n\\ndef compute_nll(probs, labels):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Compute Negative Log-Likelihood.\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    probs = torch.clamp(probs, min=1e-12, max=1.0)\\n    labels = torch.tensor(labels)\\n    nll = -torch.log(probs[torch.arange(len(labels)), labels]).mean()\\n    return nll.item()\\n\\ndef compute_brier_score(probs, labels, n_classes):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Compute Brier Score.\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    # One-hot encode labels\\n    labels_onehot = torch.zeros(len(labels), n_classes)\\n    labels_onehot.scatter_(1, torch.tensor(labels).unsqueeze(1), 1)\\n    \\n    brier = torch.mean((probs - labels_onehot) ** 2).item()\\n    return brier\\n\\ndef bootstrap_ci(metric_func, probs, labels, n_bootstrap=1000, confidence=0.95):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Compute bootstrap confidence interval for a metric.\\n    \\n    Args:\\n        metric_func: Function that computes metric\\n        probs: Predicted probabilities\\n        labels: True labels\\n        n_bootstrap: Number of bootstrap samples\\n        confidence: Confidence level\\n    \\n    Returns:\\n        (mean, lower_ci, upper_ci)\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    probs_np = probs.numpy()\\n    labels_np = np.array(labels)\\n    n = len(labels_np)\\n    \\n    bootstrap_metrics = []\\n    for _ in range(n_bootstrap):\\n        indices = np.random.choice(n, size=n, replace=True)\\n        boot_probs = probs_np[indices]\\n        boot_labels = labels_np[indices]\\n        metric = metric_func(torch.tensor(boot_probs), boot_labels)\\n        bootstrap_metrics.append(metric)\\n    \\n    bootstrap_metrics = np.array(bootstrap_metrics)\\n    mean = np.mean(bootstrap_metrics)\\n    lower = np.percentile(bootstrap_metrics, (1 - confidence) / 2 * 100)\\n    upper = np.percentile(bootstrap_metrics, (1 + confidence) / 2 * 100)\\n    \\n    return mean, lower, upper\\n```\\n\\n### Main Experiment Loop\\n```python\\ndef run_experiment(dataset_name, logits, labels, n_classes):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Run full experiment for one dataset.\\n    \\n    Args:\\n        dataset_name: Name of dataset\\n        logits: Extracted logits (N, C)\\n        labels: True labels (N,)\\n        n_classes: Number of classes\\n    \\n    Returns:\\n        Dictionary of results\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    # Split data\\n    n = len(labels)\\n    indices = np.random.permutation(n)\\n    train_idx = indices[:int(0.6 * n)]\\n    val_idx = indices[int(0.6 * n):int(0.8 * n)]\\n    test_idx = indices[int(0.8 * n):]\\n    \\n    # Prepare splits\\n    train_logits = [logits[i] for i in train_idx]\\n    train_labels = [labels[i] for i in train_idx]\\n    val_logits = [logits[i] for i in val_idx]\\n    val_labels = [labels[i] for i in val_idx]\\n    test_logits = [logits[i] for i in test_idx]\\n    test_labels = [labels[i] for i in test_idx]\\n    \\n    results = {'dataset': dataset_name}\\n    \\n    # Method 1: Uncalibrated\\n    print(f\\\"\\\\n=== {dataset_name}: Uncalibrated ===\\\")\\n    test_probs = torch.softmax(torch.tensor(test_logits), dim=-1)\\n    test_preds = torch.argmax(test_probs, dim=-1)\\n    \\n    ece = compute_ece(test_probs, test_labels)\\n    brier = compute_brier_score(test_probs, test_labels, n_classes)\\n    nll = compute_nll(test_probs, test_labels)\\n    acc = (test_preds == torch.tensor(test_labels)).float().mean().item()\\n    \\n    ece_ci = bootstrap_ci(compute_ece, test_probs, test_labels)\\n    \\n    results['uncalibrated'] = {\\n        'ece': ece,\\n        'ece_ci': ece_ci,\\n        'brier': brier,\\n        'nll': nll,\\n        'accuracy': acc\\n    }\\n    \\n    # Method 2: Temperature Scaling\\n    print(f\\\"\\\\n=== {dataset_name}: Temperature Scaling ===\\\")\\n    T_opt, val_preds, val_confs, val_probs = temperature_scaling(\\n        val_logits, val_labels, val_logits, val_labels\\n    )\\n    \\n    # Apply optimal T to test set\\n    test_scaled = torch.tensor(test_logits) / T_opt\\n    test_probs_ts = torch.softmax(test_scaled, dim=-1)\\n    test_preds_ts = torch.argmax(test_probs_ts, dim=-1)\\n    \\n    ece_ts = compute_ece(test_probs_ts, test_labels)\\n    brier_ts = compute_brier_score(test_probs_ts, test_labels, n_classes)\\n    nll_ts = compute_nll(test_probs_ts, test_labels)\\n    acc_ts = (test_preds_ts == torch.tensor(test_labels)).float().mean().item()\\n    \\n    ece_ci_ts = bootstrap_ci(compute_ece, test_probs_ts, test_labels)\\n    \\n    results['temperature_scaling'] = {\\n        'T_optimal': T_opt,\\n        'ece': ece_ts,\\n        'ece_ci': ece_ci_ts,\\n        'brier': brier_ts,\\n        'nll': nll_ts,\\n        'accuracy': acc_ts\\n    }\\n    \\n    # Method 3: TEC\\n    print(f\\\"\\\\n=== {dataset_name}: TEC ===\\\")\\n    best_params, best_ece_val = tune_tec_hyperparameters(val_logits, val_labels)\\n    T_0_opt, alpha_opt, beta_opt = best_params\\n    \\n    # Apply optimal TEC to test set\\n    test_probs_tec, test_T_sample = tec_calibration(\\n        test_logits, T_0_opt, alpha_opt, beta_opt\\n    )\\n    test_preds_tec = torch.argmax(test_probs_tec, dim=-1)\\n    \\n    ece_tec = compute_ece(test_probs_tec, test_labels)\\n    brier_tec = compute_brier_score(test_probs_tec, test_labels, n_classes)\\n    nll_tec = compute_nll(test_probs_tec, test_labels)\\n    acc_tec = (test_preds_tec == torch.tensor(test_labels)).float().mean().item()\\n    \\n    ece_ci_tec = bootstrap_ci(compute_ece, test_probs_tec, test_labels)\\n    \\n    results['tec'] = {\\n        'T_0_optimal': T_0_opt,\\n        'alpha_optimal': alpha_opt,\\n        'beta_optimal': beta_opt,\\n        'ece': ece_tec,\\n        'ece_ci': ece_ci_tec,\\n        'brier': brier_tec,\\n        'nll': nll_tec,\\n        'accuracy': acc_tec\\n    }\\n    \\n    # Heterogeneous Split Analysis\\n    print(f\\\"\\\\n=== {dataset_name}: Heterogeneous Split Analysis ===\\\")\\n    easy_idx, hard_idx = create_heterogeneous_splits(test_logits, test_labels)\\n    \\n    for split_name, split_idx in [('easy', easy_idx), ('hard', hard_idx)]:\\n        split_logits = [test_logits[i] for i in split_idx]\\n        split_labels = [test_labels[i] for i in split_idx]\\n        \\n        # Uncalibrated\\n        split_probs = torch.softmax(torch.tensor(split_logits), dim=-1)\\n        ece_split = compute_ece(split_probs, split_labels)\\n        \\n        # TS\\n        split_scaled = torch.tensor(split_logits) / T_opt\\n        split_probs_ts = torch.softmax(split_scaled, dim=-1)\\n        ece_ts_split = compute_ece(split_probs_ts, split_labels)\\n        \\n        # TEC\\n        split_probs_tec, _ = tec_calibration(\\n            split_logits, T_0_opt, alpha_opt, beta_opt\\n        )\\n        ece_tec_split = compute_ece(split_probs_tec, split_labels)\\n        \\n        results[f'heterogeneous_{split_name}'] = {\\n            'n_samples': len(split_idx),\\n            'uncalibrated_ece': ece_split,\\n            'ts_ece': ece_ts_split,\\n            'tec_ece': ece_tec_split\\n        }\\n    \\n    return results\\n```\\n\\n### Output Format\\n```python\\ndef save_results(all_results, filename='method_out.json'):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Save results to method_out.json.\\n    \\n    Format:\\n    {\\n        \\\"experiment\\\": \\\"TEC_vs_TS_evaluation\\\",\\n        \\\"datasets\\\": [\\n            {\\n                \\\"dataset\\\": \\\"sst-2\\\",\\n                \\\"n_classes\\\": 2,\\n                \\\"results\\\": {\\n                    \\\"uncalibrated\\\": {...},\\n                    \\\"temperature_scaling\\\": {...},\\n                    \\\"tec\\\": {...},\\n                    \\\"heterogeneous_easy\\\": {...},\\n                    \\\"heterogeneous_hard\\\": {...}\\n                }\\n            },\\n            ...\\n        ],\\n        \\\"summary\\\": {\\n            \\\"teec_better_than_ts_count\\\": 2,\\n            \\\"ts_better_than_teec_count\\\": 3,\\n            \\\"average_ece_improvement_ts\\\": 0.05,\\n            \\\"average_ece_improvement_tec\\\": 0.03\\n        }\\n    }\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    with open(filename, 'w') as f:\\n        json.dump(all_results, f, indent=2)\\n```\",\n  \"fallback_plan\": \"## Fallback Plan\\n\\n### Issue 1: Pre-trained Models Not Available/Fail to Load\\n**Symptoms:** Unable to load HuggingFace models, model download fails, out of memory.\\n\\n**Fallback:**\\n1. {"content": [{"cache_prompt": false, "type": "text", "text": "NOTE: We only show up to 19 since there're only 19 lines in this file.\nHere's the result of running `cat -n` on /ai-inventor/aii_data/runs/run_3fUR0i5e8NC7/3_invention_loop/iter_2/gen_plan/gen_plan_experiment_1/.sdk_openhands_agent_struct_out.json:\n     1\t{\n     2\t  \"title\": \"Test TEC vs TS Calibration on 5 LLM Datasets\",\n     3\t  \"summary\": \"Compare thermodynamic entropy calibration and temperature scaling on SST-2, QNLI, AG News, MNLI, DBpedia using pre-trained transformers. Evaluate on heterogeneous splits with bootstrap CI.\",\n     4\t  \"runpod_compute_profile\": \"gpu\",\n     5\t  \"implementation_pseudocode\": \"## Experimental Setup\\n\\n### Dataset Preparation\\n1. Load the standardized datasets from the dependency artifact (full_data_out.json)\\n2. For each dataset, load the appropriate pre-trained model:\\n   - SST-2: distilbert-base-uncased-finetuned-sst-2-english\\n   - QNLI: distilbert-base-uncased-finetuned-sst-2-english (or BERT-base)\\n   - AG News: roberta-base (fine-tuned on AG News)\\n   - MNLI: roberta-large-mnli (or roberta-base)\\n   - DBpedia: bert-base-uncased (fine-tuned on DBpedia)\\n3. Split each dataset into:\\n   - Train (60%): for model fine-tuning if needed\\n   - Validation (20%): for hyperparameter tuning\\n   - Test (20%): for final evaluation\\n\\n### Model & Logit Extraction\\n```python\\nimport torch\\nfrom transformers import AutoModelForSequenceClassification, AutoTokenizer\\nfrom torch.utils.data import DataLoader\\nimport json\\n\\n# Load dataset\\nwith open('full_data_out.json', 'r') as f:\\n    data = json.load(f)\\n\\n# Model mapping\\ndataset_models = {\\n    'sst-2': 'distilbert-base-uncased-finetuned-sst-2-english',\\n    'qnli': 'bert-base-uncased',  # May need QNLI fine-tuned version\\n    'ag_news': 'roberta-base',  # May need AG News fine-tuned\\n    'mnli': 'roberta-large-mnli',\\n    'dbpedia': 'bert-base-uncased'  # May need DBpedia fine-tuned\\n}\\n\\n# Extract logits for each dataset\\nfor dataset_name, model_name in dataset_models.items():\\n    tokenizer = AutoTokenizer.from_pretrained(model_name)\\n    model = AutoModelForSequenceClassification.from_pretrained(model_name)\\n    model.eval()\\n    \\n    # Get dataset examples\\n    dataset = [d for d in data['datasets'] if d['dataset'] == dataset_name][0]\\n    examples = dataset['examples']\\n    \\n    # Extract logits (no gradient)\\n    with torch.no_grad():\\n        for ex in examples:\\n            inputs = tokenizer(ex['input'], return_tensors='pt', truncation=True, padding=True)\\n            outputs = model(**inputs)\\n            logits = outputs.logits\\n            # Store logits with example\\n            ex['logits'] = logits.numpy().tolist()\\n            ex['num_classes'] = logits.shape[-1]\\n```\\n\\n### Method 1: Uncalibrated Baseline\\n```python\\ndef uncalibrated_predictions(logits):\\n    # Softmax without temperature scaling\\n    probs = torch.softmax(torch.tensor(logits), dim=-1)\\n    preds = torch.argmax(probs, dim=-1)\\n    confs = torch.max(probs, dim=-1).values\\n    return preds, confs, probs\\n```\\n\\n### Method 2: Temperature Scaling (TS)\\n```python\\nimport torch.nn as nn\\nimport torch.optim as optim\\n\\ndef temperature_scaling(logits, labels, val_logits, val_labels):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Tune temperature T on validation set to minimize NLL.\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    # Initialize temperature\\n    temperature = nn.Parameter(torch.ones(1) * 1.0)\\n    optimizer = optim.LBFGS([temperature], lr=0.01, max_iter=50)\\n    \\n    logits_tensor = torch.tensor(logits)\\n    labels_tensor = torch.tensor(labels)\\n    \\n    def eval():\\n        optimizer.zero_grad()\\n        scaled_logits = logits_tensor / temperature\\n        loss = nn.CrossEntropyLoss()(scaled_logits, labels_tensor)\\n        loss.backward()\\n        return loss\\n    \\n    # Optimize temperature\\n    for _ in range(100):\\n        optimizer.step(eval)\\n    \\n    # Apply to validation set\\n    with torch.no_grad():\\n        val_scaled = torch.tensor(val_logits) / temperature\\n        val_probs = torch.softmax(val_scaled, dim=-1)\\n        val_preds = torch.argmax(val_probs, dim=-1)\\n        val_confs = torch.max(val_probs, dim=-1).values\\n    \\n    return temperature.item(), val_preds, val_confs, val_probs\\n```\\n\\n### Method 3: Thermodynamic Entropy Calibration (TEC)\\n```python\\ndef compute_entropy(probs):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Compute Shannon entropy of probability distribution.\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    epsilon = 1e-12\\n    probs = torch.clamp(probs, epsilon, 1.0 - epsilon)\\n    entropy = -torch.sum(probs * torch.log(probs), dim=-1)\\n    return entropy\\n\\ndef compute_margin(probs):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Compute decision margin (difference between top-2 predictions).\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    sorted_probs, _ = torch.sort(probs, dim=-1, descending=True)\\n    margin = sorted_probs[..., 0] - sorted_probs[..., 1]\\n    return margin\\n\\ndef tec_calibration(logits, T_0, alpha, beta):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Thermodynamic Entropy Calibration.\\n    \\n    Adjusts per-sample temperature based on entropy and margin:\\n    T_sample = T_0 * (1 + alpha * entropy - beta * margin)\\n    \\n    Args:\\n        logits: Raw logits (N, C)\\n        T_0: Base temperature parameter\\n        alpha: Entropy weight parameter\\n        beta: Margin weight parameter\\n    \\n    Returns:\\n        Calibrated probabilities\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    probs = torch.softmax(torch.tensor(logits), dim=-1)\\n    entropy = compute_entropy(probs)\\n    margin = compute_margin(probs)\\n    \\n    # Normalize entropy and margin to [0, 1]\\n    max_entropy = torch.log(torch.tensor(probs.shape[-1]).float())\\n    norm_entropy = entropy / max_entropy\\n    norm_margin = margin  # Already in [0, 1]\\n    \\n    # Compute per-sample temperature\\n    T_sample = T_0 * (1 + alpha * norm_entropy - beta * norm_margin)\\n    T_sample = torch.clamp(T_sample, min=0.01, max=100.0)  # Prevent extremes\\n    \\n    # Apply temperature scaling per sample\\n    # Need to handle per-sample temperature\\n    scaled_logits = torch.tensor(logits) / T_sample.unsqueeze(-1)\\n    calibrated_probs = torch.softmax(scaled_logits, dim=-1)\\n    \\n    return calibrated_probs, T_sample\\n\\ndef tune_tec_hyperparameters(val_logits, val_labels):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Grid search for TEC hyperparameters.\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    best_ece = float('inf')\\n    best_params = None\\n    \\n    T_0_range = [0.1, 0.5, 1.0, 2.0, 5.0, 10.0, 20.0]\\n    alpha_range = [0.0, 0.5, 1.0, 1.5, 2.0]\\n    beta_range = [0.0, 0.25, 0.5, 0.75, 1.0]\\n    \\n    for T_0 in T_0_range:\\n        for alpha in alpha_range:\\n            for beta in beta_range:\\n                probs, _ = tec_calibration(val_logits, T_0, alpha, beta)\\n                ece = compute_ece(probs, val_labels)\\n                \\n                if ece < best_ece:\\n                    best_ece = ece\\n                    best_params = (T_0, alpha, beta)\\n    \\n    return best_params, best_ece\\n```\\n\\n### Heterogeneous Split Creation\\n```python\\ndef create_heterogeneous_splits(logits, labels, easy_ratio=0.5):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Split dataset into easy (high margin) and hard (low margin) examples.\\n    \\n    Args:\\n        logits: Raw logits\\n        labels: True labels\\n        easy_ratio: Ratio of easy examples to include\\n    \\n    Returns:\\n        easy_indices, hard_indices\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    probs = torch.softmax(torch.tensor(logits), dim=-1)\\n    margin = compute_margin(probs)\\n    \\n    # Sort by margin\\n    sorted_indices = torch.argsort(margin, descending=True)\\n    \\n    n_easy = int(len(sorted_indices) * easy_ratio)\\n    easy_indices = sorted_indices[:n_easy]\\n    hard_indices = sorted_indices[n_easy:]\\n    \\n    return easy_indices, hard_indices\\n```\\n\\n### Metrics Computation\\n```python\\nimport numpy as np\\nfrom sklearn.metrics import brier_score_loss\\n\\ndef compute_ece(probs, labels, n_bins=10):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Compute Expected Calibration Error.\\n    \\n    Args:\\n        probs: Predicted probabilities (N, C)\\n        labels: True labels (N,)\\n        n_bins: Number of bins for calibration\\n    \\n    Returns:\\n        ECE value\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    #
